name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Superior Twin Room
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Solo travelers
info:12 Reviews
rating:4
posted:Posted April 25, 2024
msg:Self-driving tour of the country, should be criticized and praised
As usual, let's talk about the good things first:
The hotel is in a good location, the parking lot is huge, the waiters have a strong sense of service and strong ability, and they are more straightforward and neat, which gives people a feeling of indifference, but in fact it is the illusion of high efficiency.
So, I ran into the provincial and municipal party committees meeting here.
The room is large, the decoration effect is light luxury, and the space ratio is particularly good. The big bathroom plus a big bed, the bedding is comfortable, there is no smell of smoke, and the facilities are complete. The room also delivers fruit.
Takeouts cannot be delivered to the room, you can only pick it up at the front desk. Some people may find it inconvenient. But I think this is very good. The hotel guests are well protected. Outsiders, whether they are couriers or residents who come to swim, cannot enter without a room card.
The swimming pool is very warm, and it is free for guests staying in the hotel to swim. The pool is not big and has a slight smell of stinky feet, but it is understandable.
The breakfast is delicious and hygienic.
The bad things:
The air conditioner in the room is very noisy, even at the weakest wind volume, it still buzzes. After turning it off, the room will be airtight, which is very uncomfortable. Moreover, the central air conditioner has no effect on the temperature adjus**ent in the room. It can only adjust the wind speed. The temperature will display the value but cannot affect the actual temperature of the room.
The room has only a small window and no screen. Facing the external facilities with good greenery and outdoor swimming pool, the mosquitoes in the room will be in close contact with you all night until they send you many bags and they can't eat them anymore. Don't think about fighting. Refer to the pictures and you will find that it is impossible to find them.
The most annoying facility!!! It is the induction light in the bathroom. Even if you turn it off manually, it will still light up, and the sensing distance is super long. Even if you turn over in bed, hey, it will light up. Can you imagine the feeling of being forced to be brightly illuminated when you get up to go to the toilet at night with sleepy eyes? The problem is not over yet. If the bathroom light is turned off while you are using the toilet, there is no manual switch for the bathroom near the toilet, which means that you either don't clean your PP and stick it out to let it sense again when sitting on the toilet, or clean your PP in the dark. Shouldn't the induction light in the bathroom be installed with a night light? Which smart designer taught you to install sensors on all bathroom lighting without manual operation? The problem is that they agreed and did the construction.
So, I spent a night of torture in the hot weather, unable to open the window, bitten by mosquitoes all night, and constantly illuminated by searchlights.
In addition, the deposit of this hotel is the most expensive one I have encountered in the past 10 years of self-driving across the country, which is 500 yuan. It seems that the safe bond of trust between the hotel and the guests is completely quantified by capital, and there is no service emotional card to play.
